padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1380937">laperfumamor</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-16">10/16/24 20:14</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>On me, Grand Soir is powdery at first sniff. After a few minutes the Spanish Labadum and Benzoin warm up into a heady but luxe vanilla. GS is perfect for cool weather. Not a safe blind buy due to the benzoin.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40816"comment_id="2318225"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Grand-Soir-40816.html?ccid=2318225#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2316502" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2316502" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="NOSEYBODY"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1259603"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1259603.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="NOSEYBODY" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2316502ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2316502" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.78); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1259603">NOSEYBODY</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-15">10/15/24 10:14</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Grand Soir opens all at once with notes of Spanish Labdanum, Orange, Amber, &amp; Benzoin setting the theme.<br />
<br />
The Orange note in this fragrance is interesting because It smells sweet &amp; Orangey without the Zesty Citrus, &amp; it blends seamlessly with the Spanish Labdanum between the notes of Amber &amp; Benzoin. <br />
<br />
NOTE: Amber &amp; Benzoin are close cousins. <br />
<br />
Amber smells sweet, resinous, balsamic, honey-like, caramel-like, &amp; vanilla-like, with Incense-like nuances.<br />
<br />
Benzoin smells sweet, resinous, balsamic, woody, caramel like, &amp; vanilla-like, with Cinnamon-like nuances.<br />
<br />
While the note of Amber has Labdanum it. Benzoin is often used in combination with Labdanum in Amber based fragrances.<br />
<br />
Vanilla isnt a main note, but its here supporting the entire theme of the fragrance along with the creamy, sweet, nutty, woodiness of Tonka, &amp; the Creamy woodiness of Cedar . <br />
<br />
The Lavender in this fragrance is subtle. And in combination with a note of Musk offers a soft floral/powdery nuance that adds an air of elegance &amp; sophistication to this fragrance.  <br />
<br />
Being that Grand Soir is an Amber based fragrance you'd expect it to smell Middle Eastern. But it doesnt. It smells like French Perfumery. Very demure. Very mindful...but extremely sexy.<br />
<br />
Grand Soir smells Dark Orange, Sweet, &amp; lightly spiced, like the color of its liquid. But never overly sweet. <br />
<br />
Grand Soir is not a Beast Mode fragrance. But it has a strong performance. It lingers in the air &amp; leaves a good sillage without ever being overpowering to the nose. <br />
<br />
Its the type of fragrance that forces one to look for the wearer. Because in the air it doesnt feel like its attached to anyone. It smells like its faintly everywhere.<br />
<br />
Compliment factor is very high with this one.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40816"comment_id="2316502"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Grand-Soir-40816.html?ccid=2316502#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2316442" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1712325">frankcoelho</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-15">10/15/24 09:24</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Okay, all right. This is a sleeper even with all the hype.<br />
<br />
Definitely one that brought the house to light for me. I never had much interest in others MFKs or even upper echelon niche, until this came in. It has everything I'd need, in the right bottle size, and to be honest for a fair price (still expensive).<br />
<br />
Opens with a bright orange smell, surrounded by this semi-resinous already scent. It stays rather "fresh" for the first 15min or so and then the mid-base starts pushing heavier than the bright aromatics. Vanillic, ambary (we all know this), and particularly the benzoin - thankfully overly powdery from the tonka - dominate very linearly the remainder of the life of the fragrance. This will last all they way, well over 9-10h on skin and very noticeable.<br />
<br />
Explaining my decision in buying it. Went in blindly, of course after watching reviews, etc. A big deal came up for $185 on the 70ml/2.4oz full pres, and I had my eye on it. Other friends were wanting me to try and I took the chance. No regrets.<br />
Great performance, without any absurd projection, but I were 3 other fragrances yesterday and GS was the most prominent (for comparison, NY Nights, Noir Extreme, and Layton were the fragrances). I'd love to see this for $150 but happy with the purchase, definitely.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40816"comment_id="2316442"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Grand-Soir-40816.html?ccid=2316442#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2315788" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2280709">Luciscool18</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-08">10/08/24 15:10</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>MFK Grand Soir is a very complicated fragrance, not in terms of notes but in terms of actually understanding what you're smelling I blind bought this fragrance for $240 and I must say it was a very big letdown when I looked at the accords and saw vanilla, Amber, powdery, and sweet. I was just about all in on it already and then I looked at the notes and they looked perhaps even better with some of my favorite notes in it with the amber and the vanilla and even orange in it, which I thought could maybe even give it a better touch perhaps smelling like a cream sickle it made me believe. Oh how I was wrong it didn't take very long to get from Paris to my house and when I tell you, how excited I was when I first saw this, it would be an understatement if I could describe it. But when I smelled it my ear to ear smile that you would see on a kid on Christmas morning quickly disappeared. I was expecting an explosion of Amber and vanilla to bless my nostrils, but what I got was an overpowering earthy powdery smelling orange with no sign of vanilla or Amber anywhere. I seriously kept smelling it and could not pick up a trace of vanilla or Amber the two top accords weren't even in the fragrance. Grand soar has been sitting on my shelf for a very long time and I've had it for about two or three months and it may be worn it three times and I wear cologne every single day. I will say the bottle in the packaging is a great presentation, but it lacks an actual smell. I had such high hopes for this fragrance, but it just didn't live up to the hype. And by no means is this fragrance bad it's just not the mind blowing can't miss smell that I thought it was.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40816"comment_id="2309242"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Grand-Soir-40816.html?ccid=2309242#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2306766" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1094278">Trendkill97</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-06">10/06/24 09:27</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>King of modern ambers. Shimmery, cozy, smooth, warm, addictive, luxurious. Though it's a tough job, Francis Kurkdjian has mastered this kind of scent profile ensuring it being not too sweet, not too cloying. Ingredients of benzoin, orange and labdanum is worked really well by this house Amyris is another subtle elusive stunner, for instance (not that it smells anything like GS). A close, inviting scent bubble, instantly elevates your presence, a scent whose whiffs are to be discovered, defining the aura of the wearer. Top tier for good reason from MFK.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40816"comment_id="2306766"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Grand-Soir-40816.html?ccid=2306766#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2306377" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2306377" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Captain Odour"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1506569"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1506569.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Captain Odour" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Amyris-Homme-Extrait-de-Parfum-59744.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.59744.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Amyris Homme Extrait de Parfum"title="Amyris Homme Extrait de Parfum"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2306377ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2306377" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.9); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1506569">Captain Odour</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-05">10/05/24 21:23</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>It's excellent. I very much like olfactorysettings review below mine, describing it as reminiscent of a furniture/antique store, because that's an apt description.<br />
<br />
Grand Soir is a remarkable fragrance in that in spite of it being so linear, it still remains intriguing. It's an Amber and Benzoin fragrance, but the people who describe it as a "bomb" are, at least in my opinion, not quite right. It's surprisingly subtle. It has monstrous longevity and excellent projection, but this isn't a slap in the face like some other fragrances. To me, Grand Soir does something that very few cooler weather scents can do well. It presents itself with warmth and coziness as one would hope for, but still maintains enough airiness and space within the fragrance that it isn't cloying or overbearing. Some would call me a "sissy sprayer," but I've always subscribed to the ethos that a good fragrance should be discovered and not announced. <br />
<br />
I know people who have gone through 3 bottles of this fragrance, and I find it hard to blame them. It's addicting. I have a very hard time not smelling myself when I'm wearing it, because it's just that good. I'll let others harp on the notes and how the various accords create this fragrance. I'm not a perfumer, and in the grand scheme of things I'm basically a caveman that goes "ugg ugg, smelly good." With that said, this is an excellent fragrance that deserves much of the praise it gets. Will I burn through 3 bottles anytime soon? I severely doubt it. But I'm eagerly looking forward to cooler weather so that I can get Grand Soir into my rotation more heavily.<br />
<br />
I usually touch on the price last in my reviews. I think it's relatively reasonable, at least when compared to some other houses. Not naming names, but it's French and rhymes with Greed. I wouldn't call this blind buy safe, but it's close to it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40816"comment_id="2306377"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Grand-Soir-40816.html?ccid=2306377#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2305060" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1588494">Ninamariah</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-29">09/29/24 01:11</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This perfume doesn’t need to be introduced anymore since it’s loved by so many and there is so many reviews on this iconic beauty. It deserves anyway all the attention since it's one of the best in the market in it's category.<br />
<br />
This is the most beautiful Amber Vanilla I know. The smell is luxurious which I can’t say of many gourmand leaning scents. I don’t even think this as a gourmand despite Vanilla is so prominent here. It heels quite linear scent but there is a depth and complexity which has been blended so perfectly into the pleasant and crowd pleasing form. It never disappoints me and I think I will never get bored with this. The overall feeling is golden and bright, luminous and resinous. I didn’t have it for a while since my last bottle was finished and few weeks ago I got a new bottle. This a must have Amber scent but it can be too spicy for many so sample it first. This is the best from the house together with Oud Satin Mood, at least for me . 💯💎<br />
<br />
The scent is totally unisex, the sillage is irresistible and huge like is the scent bubble around the wearer. It has already became a classic and the reputation it carries is fully deserved.<br />
<br />
About the main ingredients (edited and simplified from the original presentation of the ingredients):<br />
<br />
Tonka bean from Brazil and Venezuela gradually develops its flavors, including those of its main aromatic molecule, coumarin: powdery, almondy with a freshly mown hay effect, tobacco, slightly honeyed and smoked. Vanilla Amber accord here include two main ingredients: Spanish labdanum (Cistus Labdanum), with its warm, resinous, animal facets, and vanillin which is a new, sweet aromatic compound and it is the primary component of vanilla. The smell of benzoin from Siam here is multi-faceted. It's like sweet Vanilla, with a gourmand caramel effect, honeyed, syrupy. It's not overly sweet though. Cistus could be extracted in several ways. The steam distillation of its branches yields the aromatic Extraction with volatile solvents results in the heavier cistus-labdanum absolute, at once balsamy, pyrogenic and resinous, used in the heart and base of a fragrance. Lavender for me can be very difficult note and luckily it's aromatic, fresh, herbaceous, camphorated and aniseed oil doesn't perform here strongly, it's barely noticeable, polished into the silky, smooth, gentle sophistication. <br />
<br />
Thank you for reading and I would appreciate a lot if you want to follow me on IG: @ninamariah_perfumes</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40816"comment_id="2298646"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Grand-Soir-40816.html?ccid=2298646#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2297416" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1558761">autumnjoy</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-25">09/25/24 10:49</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Sugary-sweet amber, very sheer and light and golden. It’s fine but not even close to being worth the price tag and it’s also not very interesting. But my taste is rather gothic so take that with a grain of salt lol</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40816"comment_id="2294757"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Grand-Soir-40816.html?ccid=2294757#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2294126" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2294126" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Carlitos"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1071323"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1071323.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Carlitos" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Elixir-68415.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.68415.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Sauvage Elixir"title="Sauvage Elixir"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2294126ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2294126" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.83); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1071323">Carlitos</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-24">09/24/24 19:13</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>WHAT A GREAT EVENING !<br />
<br />
The wind had almost stopped. The sails were practily useless so we just turned the motor on at low revs, just to have the impression of really gaining some knots against the river current.<br />
The sky perfectly mimicked Van Gogh's "Starry Night". Although in Sowthern Egypt the Nile current was always detectable, the surface looked like a black serene mirror. Due to a lot of talk about the local deities of bygone days, I couldn't help but think that Maat ruled this night at her pleasure. The Goddess responsible for maintaining the cosmic order was giving us a glimpse of her power through a profoundly calm and silent night. Only the tuk-tuk-tuk of the engine broke that reigning peace.<br />
I was always very curious about the Nubian transition from Cairo to non-humanized Egypt, always scrutinizing the surface of the water in the secret desire to catch a glimpse of the whirlpool caused by a crocodile. Salah, one of the local crew members, had already discouraged me several times with a disdainful smile: “Sahib Carlos, stop dreaming. You'll get lucky only after Aswan.”<br />
We finally spotted the village where we wanted to drop anchor and stay the night. To our amazement, a luminous aura, artificially yellowed, covered the village of less than 50 houses that bordered the Nile right bank. A dozen children jumped onto the small pier shouting with joy at the sight of unexpected rich visitors... and gazed in amazement at the various men and women wearing shorts with their legs showing. They later informed us that the local Iman had bought an eletric generator. The right bank of the Nubian Nile was absolutely dark due to the total absence of any modern infrastructure. This village was the sole exception, although we ignored it at the time. Once a week, a small night market was held here, bringing together almost two hundred people in the small central square. All this was possible thanks to the miracle of electric light - not much, but enough to cheer the soul. Luck was on our side when we arrived on the night of the village fair. After all, we weren't going to sleep for a long while.<br />
We went as a group to the small, illuminated central square. The group quickly turned into a procession with dozens of children hopping around us.<br />
The technological miracle of several incandescent bulbs allowed about twenty sales tents to spread out in meticulous disarray. The couple of hundred people circulating there all fell silent at our arrival. But their astonishment soon passed. Not only had the children announced our arrival, but it was much more interesting to continue the gossip and haggling, which were just as important as the business itself.<br />
I wasn't surprised by the few objects that confirmed Egypt as a land of tourists. I just didn't see any tourists apart from us. I quickly forgot the few t-shirts with clumsy hieroglyphics, but made of good cotton, and the dozen or so stone scarabs, painted green or turquoise, which, for me, were still responsible for creating this country. My nose dragged my eyes to the stand full of yellow benzoin stones next to another pile of black labdanum stones. The next stand displayed spices, with vanilla and reddish-yellow saffron in heaps, as well as bags of dried flowers of which I only recognized lavender. There was more variety of resins and incense, but I couldn't recognize even half of what was on sale.<br />
Everywhere there were small burners to demonstrate the excellence of the “bakoors”, but all the strands of smoke were tangled together. At a distance of one meter, I could only smell the intoxicating aroma of that spontaneous mixture. To take it with us, we would certainly have to buy a wide variety of resins and spices. Yet the smell was vaguely familiar. It was clearly sweet and resinous, but the scents of lavender and vanilla seemed perfectly intertwined with the burning resins.<br />
Each tent had its own olfactory footprint. Where citronella was also burned, the smell was more alimony. Where there were bags of pepper and cloves, the smell was sometimes fresher and sometimes earthier. But my favorite tent only had benzoin, labdanum, lavender and vanilla. The more I smelled “my store”, the more that vanilla-amber scent suggested images of the luxuries from the 1001 Nights. That scent was well stored in my memory bank. I just couldn't put a name tag on it. I had already come across that fragrance several times that perfectly combined sweetness and resins. It was then that one of my travel companions, François, a worthy representative of the Gallic language on that adventure, crossed my path. Amid laughter and camaraderie, he exclaimed:<br />
- “Mais quel soir!... Quel Grand Soir!"  (What an evening!... What a Great Evening!)<br />
<br />
The scent<br />
Grand Soir is one of those fragrances that you have to give full attention to in order to experience its transcendental effect. When you fully concentrate on Grand Soir's scent you reach an olfactory almost meditative state. Hardly any other perfume manages to captivate me so completely. Grand Soir is a feeling and a life experience by itself.<br />
This perfume is more than just a perfume. It is a sensual work of art that seduces the senses and briefely touches the soul. The fragrance opens with an explosion of resinous notes accompanied by sweet notes. Later, the resinous notes blend with the purest amber and a hearty vanilla, providing a deep and lasting warmth. Behind the scent design is Kurkdjian's vision to create a feeling of opulence and elegance that reflects people's dreams and desires. The fragrance is a tribute to the beauty and magic of the evening in particular, It is a hommage to the hours when everything is possible and the world seems easy to reach with your hand.<br />
My nose tells me benzoin, amber, vanilla and tonka. As the fragrance progresses, it becomes slightly more vanilic. Otherwise, there's no real changeability or progression. But I don't think that's bad at all.<br />
This fragrance is the epitome of warm harmony. There's nothing more to say. This fragrance is not complex. It's simple. And sometimes, simplicity is the highest form of perfection.<br />
<br />
My opinion:<br />
Grand Soir is an expensive fragrance that you should not buy blindly. You may be one of those rare sould that is prone to deslike this perfume.<br />
Also forget about its gender. Is it masculine or feminine? This is both for me. One day it seems completely unisex, another day it seems striking and masculine. Sometimes when I'm wearing the perfume, it smells simply sensual, feminine and smooth.<br />
As a man, I simply smell educated, charming, sensitive, confidente, determined and happy. If I wanted to get all these feelings in therapy sessions, I would certainly spend a lot more money and get fewer results.<br />
<br />
Music:<br />
Topol - "If I Were A Rich Man"<br />
or<br />
Aram Khachaturian - "Adagio of Spartacus and Phrygia" from the ballet Spartacus</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40816"comment_id="2294126"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Grand-Soir-40816.html?ccid=2294126#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2293220" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Kind of reminds me of CK Obsession for Men - an extremely elevated version, that is - freed from some of the heavy spices which added to its masculinity but also made it not so approachable and kind of old man-ish smelling. This, on the other hand, feels rounder, more modern, more elegant, richer, easier to wear and totally unisex. Excellent quality overall. Not a signature type scent for me, but a great fragrance for special occasions during Autumn and Winter. It stays true to itself as it dries down and it performs great, both in projection and longevity. Probably my favorite MFK out of the ones I've tested.<br />

It smells initially extremely!!! masculine, woodier and more aromatic than I wanted, but overall still a gorgeous smell (it smells expensive, sorry to be a snob but its true you can smell the quality sometimes). <br />
<br />
The dry down is where I start to fall in love, its incredibly smooth and sweet, woody and complex. On my third wear I realised I was really enjoying the smell wafting up at me 5 hours later after spraying (twice, one on wrist one on back of neck) and have since grown to love it even more. <br />
<br />
I am a hoe for vanilla, absolute basic bitch, I just want to smell deliciously feminine and edible, which this DOES give me (especially after an hour or two), but its also a little more complicated than that and I will be buying a FB to get to know better through winter :)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2275947" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Cosmos_PMF"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2108424"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2108424.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Cosmos_PMF" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Xerjoff/Torino22-77059.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.77059.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Torino22"title="Torino22"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2275947ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2275947" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.78); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2108424">Cosmos_PMF</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-08">09/08/24 10:59</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is the best date night fragrance ever. Gold medal in straight-forward amber scents out there.<br />
<br />
I remember I entered a boutique in my city with had a lot of niche brands and the main selling category there was the brand of Maison Francis Kurkdjian, the master perfumer. I smelled a few fragrances from the cap (like BR540, oud satin mood, gentle fluidity line) and all of them really had something in common which I found really addicting.<br />
I first tested Grand Soir on my skin and man, it was radiant, warm and really sophisticated. Before buying it I know I kept testing it in other european cities next to other tested colognes to see if I'm really gonna purchase the bottle of this one. Everytime I had even 3 to 6 legendary fragrances on my arm, I kept choosing Grand soir because it was the one that always stood out. <br />
I finally went into the official website of MFK and purchased the classy looking 35ml bottle with 3 other complimentary samples. <br />
<br />
Talking about the scent profile, this is a simple, very french smelling amber-sweet-floral with a special touch of warmth sophisticated fragrance. The opening is absolutely gorgeous and luxurious smelling. Floral powdery. In the entire process of the fragrance (which is pretty linear) you pick up the beautiful vanilla-amber combo supported by the sexy done of benzoin in the background. Pretty gourmand. Once you hit the dry down in some hours the nose is tickled by the soft spices that come from the tonka bean. And in the last hour of the longevity I actually get chocolate nuances. Extremely smooth, this keeps you in that bubble of french smelling well crafted perfumery, excellent blend of notes for sure. You will smell wealthy, confident and well put together.<br />
<br />
Talking about performance this is the fragrance' unique part. Longevity is 12hrs+ but with soft to moderate projection. Crafted for a seductive date night scent, it's that type of fragrance which is discovered by the special people and not announced. Definetly not loud beast mode.<br />
<br />
Versatility of occasions to wear Grand soir is pretty tricky. Personally I would wear this in special events only and in formal attires. Not a casual scent at all to be worn around school or clubbing around. This is a very warm scent even though you could get away with it during spring nights too. The translation of "Grand Soir" means "The Big Night", so it makes sense. Could be used in the daytime special occassions too.<br />
Gender-wise, both genders can wear this and every age group can rock this. It's an elegant smell for everyone.<br />
This scent should be worn to create memories, in short.<br />
<br />
I see myself taking the bottle with me as an accessory in my suit pocket. You're gonna get compliments on the 35ml slim bottle besides the scent itself. Amazing cap similar to Xerjoff's, smooth gliding and of course, perfect pressurized atomizer. Very good in details. <br />
<br />
MFK has become one of my favourite niche houses ever. I'm also a big fan of Oud satin mood and BR540 edp/extrait. Grand soir is my favourite from the brand<br />
<br />
Maison Francis Kurkdjian Grand Soir: simple and formal dressed up french sweet amber vanilla floral scent. The ultimate date night fragrance. Warm and inviting. Eternal lasting. The person who wears this fragrance will be named as "wealthy", "classy", "high status", "classy man/woman". Sophistication for everyone. Definetly a 10/10.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40816"comment_id="2275947"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Grand-Soir-40816.html?ccid=2275947#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2272867" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Longevity: 7/10<br />

Price: 4/10<br />

Smells strongly of vanilla extract with spicy resinous notes.  Doesn’t change much as you wear it, just fades with the same notes start to finish. Not overly sweet to my taste and something cozy for yourself or when someone is in your bubble. It’s definitely quality, but on the fence if it is worth the price compared to other ambers.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40816"comment_id="2239370"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Grand-Soir-40816.html?ccid=2239370#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2238530" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; The dry down is very nice and I can see why the fragrance is loved but personally I can’t get past the opening</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40816"comment_id="2238530"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Grand-Soir-40816.html?ccid=2238530#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2237740" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2237740" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="FreshLiving"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1043744"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1043744.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="FreshLiving" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Creed/Royal-Oud-12317.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.12317.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Royal Oud"title="Royal Oud"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2237740ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2237740" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.81); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1043744">FreshLiving</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-03">08/03/24 10:46</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>For the past month I’ve been experiencing Maison Francis Kurkdjian fragrances and it’s honestly been an enriching journey. First things first, the man knows how to blend a fragrance, even if that particular scent isn’t for me. All his juices are so refined, complex, and smell of someone wealthy. <br />
<br />
When I first started out with MFK I read Grand Soir was Amber and vanilla; which aren’t necessarily my favourites. So I did overlook this and had only sniffed Grand Soir very casually from the lid and atomizer, as when I first saw it in-person I figured it was a females fragrance, as the amber bottles with gold accents usually seem to be for females. <br />
<br />
Yesterday I found myself sampling it; the sales associate who was thirsty for a sale started spraying all the fragrances on smelling cards. When he sprayed this I was immediately intrigued and shocked. Shocked that this is the fragrance I had not tested yet, and intrigued because the scent was very different than what I had expected. He went on to romance the fragrance speaking of a night Paris and booze accords, rich and opulent and did a great job with the description. And honestly.. it was exactly what I was smelling and could envision the experience. It’s how wealthy smells during a black tie event at an estate. <br />
<br />
This is a terrific fragrance. It’s sexy, sensual, mature, perfect amount of sweetness to smokiness, and leaning more classy masculine, without being overbearing. The spice here is absolutely sublime. <br />
<br />
It lasts a long time (still going on 14 hours here), projects well and for about 4-5 hours with the right amount you’d want in a fragrance.<br />
<br />
I think this is best suited for formal events, live shows, dinner dates, and evenings. Something where you are there to feel swanky. Can be worn in Winter, Fall, early Spring season nights.<br />
<br />
Masculine Pluriel is the James Bond fragrance. That’s his signature. Grand Soir is what he wears when he’s in a tux at an event and being smooth as hell while he gets the girl. <br />
<br />
Just purchased my bottle! And my only critique on MFK is I wish their bottle options came in 70ml, 125ml, then 200ml<br />
70 and 200 are way too big of a gap. <br />
<br />
And to those who thinks this js grandfatherly or bohemian? I just don’t see that at all. No way.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40816"comment_id="2237740"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Grand-Soir-40816.html?ccid=2237740#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2237241" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
Grand Soir is the most simple fragrance of its archetype, contemporaries simply do not do it as well. Given my propensity for enjoying vanillas and ambers I naturally love Grand Soir. I will say I believe that it features the single best vanilla I’ve ever smelled, the vanilla evolved from creamy almost akin to an ice cream to the husk and a more bitter vanilla. As for the amber, it is deep and resinous and complex while complimenting the vanilla perfectly. The other notes I detect are lavender and a slight licorice like accord I believe is from the labdanum, however both are really only present for about a hour.<br />
<br />
Longevity- 10/10<br />
Smell - 10/10<br />
Versatility - 3/10<br />
Projection - Nuke<br />
<br />
Total 9/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40816"comment_id="2232263"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Grand-Soir-40816.html?ccid=2232263#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2232034" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2226571" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="hatsumomo23"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1886692"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1886692.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="hatsumomo23" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Nishane/Ani-X-80464.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.80464.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Ani X"title="Ani X"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2226571ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2226571" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.71); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1886692">hatsumomo23</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-22">07/22/24 20:50</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Grand Soir is a fragrance I reach for when I want attention. The fun thing about finding your literal niche with fragrance is when you find one that reinforces how you want to feel about yourself and how you want to come off to other people. Grand Soir does that for me. It’s strong. It’s dark. It’s kind of sexy without trying so hard. An established sexy. The kind of person that doesn’t have to say too much. The quiet Daddy, if you will. He looks good and knows how to dress. The scent of a gentleman on a date. He’s not trying to impress or seduce you. Don’t get me wrong, I love a first date fragrance like say Eros Flame, but this is ‘Salt and Pepper’ sexy. I’m not saying that a younger person couldn’t pull this off, but I am saying that it takes a confident individual with a little sex appeal to make this work: <br />
 That energy isn’t going to come from someone freshly 21. <br />
More on the actual scent itself:<br />
There’s cinnamon in this. It’s not listed in most places, but on the official site, it’s the first note they talk about.<br />
It’s pretty linear, but what you’re getting the entire time is what I’m pretty sure you’re looking for, so it’s kind of fantastic in that way. The juice color really does match the scent. That ambery warm orange is perfect for this. I’m at a stage in my fragrance journey where I’m less concerned about the time of year and more interested in how I feel that day when I’m applying a scent. The atomizer on this bottle is great because I can just do two half sprays of this while in any weather condition and be absolutely fine.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1673973">ethan-fragrantica</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-19">07/19/24 06:55</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Grand Soir by Maison Francis Kurkdjian:<br />
Warm and high quality, there is definitely more to it than vanilla and amber, the benzoin stands out as a dry resinous note and the labdanum is detectable too. The tonka then makes everything slightly creamier and smoother. I could see myself wearing it occasionally but it's more suited to older guys. Could be a cold weather signature, it has good performance. I think it's more nuanced than people give it credit for and is just a nice sophisticated scent. <br />
<br />
Notes: Vanilla, amber, labdanum, benzoin, tonka<br />
<br />
Longevity: 4.5/5<br />
Sillage: 4/5<br />
Scent: 3/5<br />
Design: 4/5<br />
Gender: Masculine<br />
Overall: 4/5</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40816"comment_id="2223263"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Grand-Soir-40816.html?ccid=2223263#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2221375" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I find it to be bitter, medicinal and overly-spiced. I purchased a bottle thinking it would grow on me as everyone raved about it, but I still found it to be unbearable- even in the later drydown. While perfume is subjective, I whole heartedly believe that anyone that's gotten their nose on other heavy hitter ambers such as Akkad, Ambre Nuit, or Ambra Aurea to name a few- would likely still NOT rank Grand Soir as a top amber perfume.<br />
<br />
MFK in general is a nice mainstream entry-level-niche house, and I respect Francis Kurkdjian's work particularly in other houses such as Indult. But once you get your nose on other niche/indie work it is hard to circle back to MFK - the exception being Oud Mood line which is spectacular.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40816"comment_id="2218801"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Grand-Soir-40816.html?ccid=2218801#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2218330" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2218330" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Bread6602"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2148915"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2148915.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Bread6602" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2218330ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2218330" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.81); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2148915">Bread6602</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-14">07/14/24 08:38</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>MFK Grand Soir is a very well known fragrance. I was very excited to try this fragrance. Grand Soir is a very nice vanilla fragrance. It opens with a heavy dose of amber with vanilla floating in the background. Then the vanilla starts to come to the forefront and brings some floral notes with it. The fragrance is very nice. However, there is a old man smell lingering in the background that I can't shake. I do not know what creates it but for me it makes the fragrance a like and not a love. <br />
<br />
With this being said, I do love the vanilla in Grand Soir though. The vanilla combined with the rich amber is a heavenly sent which unfortunately is disturbed by the old man smell. The only other fragrance with a more prestigious vanilla is YSL Babycat. If you also did not love Grand Soir but still have a craving for a vanilla fragrance I would recommend trying YSL Babycat. I also wrote a review on that fragrance. <br />
<br />
This fragrance does have incredible longevity and projection. This would stay on clothes for months if you never washed them. Easily 10+ hours of great projection. 2-3 Sprays and you will fill every room you walk into. This scent is perfect for a formal event as it is very mature. <br />
<br />
Longevity: 10/10<br />
Projection: 10/10<br />
Smell: 7/10<br />

padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2201921" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Fortyfree"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1631067"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1631067.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Fortyfree" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2201921ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2201921" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.78); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1631067">Fortyfree</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-28">06/28/24 06:51</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Sweet, delicious gourmand.<br />
<br />
Opens with a rich cinnamon aroma, it's a little dark and woody.<br />
It's also warm and creamy, with a sweet aura of something that smells like "milky-tea."<br />
A true gourmand scent that has many edible facets, smells a bit like a "Pecan Plait" or "Caramel Latte."<br />
It's nutty and has some rose maybe? Has plenty of vanilla too.<br />
Malty, toffee, treacle. Becomes "lactonic" but still resembles a French bakery. Some wafts of honey as well.<br />
After an hour it becomes a little aromatic, remains woody and has some patchouli underneath. <br />
Vanilla is still present alongside notes of butterscotch, the scent remains milky and creamy.<br />
Gets a little bit earthy as it turns to a skin scent. <br />
<br />
This is a high quality, opulent scent that would work best for formal occasions in the autumn or during the winter. <br />
<br />
It lasts as a skin scent until the next day, but other performance (Projection etc.) is hard to gauge. <br />
<br />
I like it and it's a very addictive skin scent, certainly in the first few hours.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40816"comment_id="2201921"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Grand-Soir-40816.html?ccid=2201921#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2199507" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1807665">AndyMomTom</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-25">06/25/24 18:20</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>It has a very quality ambery and vanilla scent. However, I am not a fan of the benzoin smell. To me, it makes the perfume smell slightly musty.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40816"comment_id="2199507"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Grand-Soir-40816.html?ccid=2199507#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2199417" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2199417" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="skibidisigma77"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2177199"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2177199.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="skibidisigma77" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2199417ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2199417" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.71); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2177199">skibidisigma77</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-25">06/25/24 15:54</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This smells really nice, a very good vanilla amber fragrance.<br />
However, if your looking for a nice creamy amber vanilla for a way better price that in my opinion genuinely smells better than grand soir, I'd go for L'Occitane Ambre. It's much cheaper, it doesn't perform as well, but only by a little, and you can always just spray more, it would be cheaper than buying a full bottle of grand soir. For a much lower price point and a better smelling scent that only lasts a little less, I'd say the choice is obvious.<br />
Grand soir is still a very nice fragrance of course, if you have the money and you love the smell, you can do whatever you want.<br />
<br />
8/10, nice high quality simple scent.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40816"comment_id="2199417"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Grand-Soir-40816.html?ccid=2199417#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2198391" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2198391" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="fragranceking12345"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2176241"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="fragranceking12345" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2198391ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2198391" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.81); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2176241">fragranceking12345</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-24">06/24/24 16:00</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>When it comes to evoking the splendor of a grand evening in Paris, Maison Francis Kurkdjian’s Grand Soir captures the essence with remarkable finesse. This luxurious scent, a creation of the esteemed perfumer Francis Kurkdjian, is a masterclass in warmth, elegance, and sophistication.<br />
<br />
Opening Notes:<br />
<br />
The fragrance opens with a lavish embrace of amber and vanilla. From the first spritz, the amber provides a golden, honeyed warmth that feels both inviting and opulent. The vanilla, far from being overly sweet, adds a creamy smoothness that perfectly balances the richness of the amber.<br />
<br />
Heart Notes:<br />
<br />
As the fragrance develops, the heart reveals itself with the introduction of benzoin from Siam. This note adds a balsamic, slightly spicy sweetness that deepens the fragrance, making it more complex and intriguing. The benzoin lends a comforting, almost nostalgic quality to the scent, reminiscent of ancient resins and exotic locales.<br />
<br />
Base Notes:<br />
<br />
The dry down of Grand Soir is where the fragrance truly shines. Tonka bean and cistus labdanum form the base, providing a deeply resinous, slightly smoky finish. The tonka bean brings a sweet, almond-like undertone, while the labdanum contributes a rich, leathery depth. Together, they create a lingering, sophisticated trail that exudes confidence and elegance.<br />
<br />
Longevity and Sillage:<br />
<br />
In terms of performance, Grand Soir excels. It is a long-lasting fragrance, with the rich, warm notes lingering on the skin for hours. The sillage is moderate to heavy, ensuring that the scent makes a statement without overwhelming the senses. This makes it an ideal choice for evening wear and special occasions, where you want your presence to be felt and remembered.<br />
<br />
Season and Occasion:<br />
<br />
Grand Soir is best suited for the cooler months of fall and winter, when its warm, enveloping notes can be fully appreciated. It is a perfect companion for formal events, romantic evenings, and any occasion that calls for a touch of elegance and sophistication. Picture a night out in Paris, dressed to the nines, with the city's lights reflecting off the Seine – that's the essence of Grand Soir.<br />
<br />
Final Thoughts:<br />
<br />
Maison Francis Kurkdjian’s Grand Soir is more than just a fragrance; it’s an experience. It tells a story of opulence and timeless elegance, making you feel like you’ve stepped into a grand evening in the heart of Paris. For those who appreciate complex, warm, and luxurious scents, Grand Soir is a must-have in your collection. It’s a testament to Francis Kurkdjian’s skill as a perfumer and his ability to create fragrances that are both memorable and deeply emotive.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; To put it very simply, it smells like warm skin on a cold winter night. To be less direct, it is a beautiful blend that is pretty much pure amber with slight added sweetness and a burnt edge, which is most evident in the opening.  Fairly linear, but with a fragrance like this it does not need to be non-linear. Greatness in a bottle, Heaven in a bottle. It is all true. The only caveat is, it is lacking something. Something else. It is a great scent, one of if not the best, but that one factor,<br />
<br />
<br />
<br />
<br />
<br />
<br />
<br />
Doesn't hurt it at all XD</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40816"comment_id="2180455"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Grand-Soir-40816.html?ccid=2180455#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2177352" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2140989">Om3r_perfumes</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-29">05/29/24 11:30</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Currently Grand soir is one of my favorite perfumes! It’s the only perfume I nearly finished. At first when I purchased it I never thought it would be in my top 5, however after time I just fell in love with this fragrance. The powerful amber and vanilla notes make this fragrance a joy to smell. It’s a perfect scent to use during the winter and fall. It projects a good distance and lasts for above 12 hours. The amber note makes it slightly different to normal vanilla scents in the market making it more attractive. There isn’t anything negative to say, MFK’s Grand Soir doesn’t come at an extremely high price point either. For a niche perfume at this quality and with this popularity its value isn’t too bad. Overall, paying this price you’re getting something for its value. It lasts long, it’s definitely a compliment getter and has good projection. I do recommend to buy this fragrance, and even for a blind buy I would say it’s quite safe to do so. I haven’t met anyone who hate this perfume.<br />
<br />
Scent: 10<br />
Projection: 9<br />
Longevity: 10<br />
Value: 8<br />
Overall: 9.5</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40816"comment_id="2171486"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Grand-Soir-40816.html?ccid=2171486#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2171086" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
Grand Soir was the first niche fragrance I purchased at full retail. When I first sniffed it, I was underwhelmed. It quickly grew on me and became my signature for a while. It holds a special place in my heart as I wore it the first time I met my now girlfriend, to which she was quick to complement. I've had 3 bottles, however; none smell exactly the way my first bottle did. My first bottle had more vanilla, and smelled better blended. Not saying that the current formulations don't smell good, they just simply do not smell the same. To my nose, the new formulations have less vanilla and more lavender. Overall, good fragrance; worth the price. <br />
<br />
Rating: 7/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40816"comment_id="2145781"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Grand-Soir-40816.html?ccid=2145781#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2145190" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I love a bold, smoldering, amber fragrance, that being said, I smelled like a man. I really wanted to love it but I couldn't lie to myself, there's just too much wood. It's so sexy......for a man, in my opinion.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40816"comment_id="2137676"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Grand-Soir-40816.html?ccid=2137676#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2131917" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Longish-lasting with decent sillage.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40816"comment_id="2128741"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Grand-Soir-40816.html?ccid=2128741#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2128596" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
I tried this perfume 2 years ago and quickly discarded it; it was too masculine and somehow synthetic. I never finished the sample and retried it a few days ago and WOWWW, it was totally different. I could smell the vanilla, the lavender, and a bit of smokiness. Even if the notes are very simple, somehow this perfume seems different, more elegant, more upscale.<br />
<br />

Longevity is excellent, sillage moderate and the scent is fairly linear.<br />
A tiny bit of sweetness, loads of warmth from the dominant amber, vanilla, a touch of wood (sandalwood?) and smoothness. Smoothness, smoothness, smoothness.<br />
I think it would suit all genders!<br />
<br />
Edit: Ugh, it's so good for layering, l can't even... Grand Soir is just so useful.<br />
<br />
Edit 2: Still love it, though the people around me seem not to. To be fair, though, where I live people prefer fresh, clean scents. Grand Soir is NOT fresh and Clean. It's warm, cozy and a mouthful of creamyness. Oh well, too bad for them that I hate fresh, clean scents.
