padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1610243" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="MrMrOverHere"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1260156"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1260156.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="MrMrOverHere" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Nasomatto/Pardon-12130.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.12130.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Pardon"title="Pardon"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1610243ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck8x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1610243" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.85); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1260156">MrMrOverHere</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-07-25">07/25/22 10:05</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>There are some fragrance categories that I no longer gravitate toward as a consumer, not because I no longer enjoy scents of that type, but specifically because I've purchased a fragrance that, to my nose, is the best possible example of its particular classification, and I'm just not interested in trying to improve upon it. For me, in the case of ambers, Grand Soir is that fragrance. <br />
<br />
It's what I think of as "textbook" in the genre, and quite apart from my usual preferences, it's completely safe, not particularly daring or dark, unchallenging, and has zero rough edges, but even still, it has more or less closed the door on amber scents for my foreseeable future. And I'm okay with that. There is admittedly something sort of bittersweet to the arrival of that moment since it means that a particular leg of the fragrance journey has come to a close, but ultimately I think it's really important to take a step back every now and then to admit when you're completely satisfied with something. The term "holy grail" gets tossed around far too much in these instances, and I think descriptions like that turn a collecting hobby into something more serious than it needs to be. I'd offer up "finish line" instead.<br />
<br />
GS is a syrupy amber, which is what I gravitate toward. It feels as though you're dripping in amber. However, that may not be the specific vibe you're looking for, and if that's the case, more power to you. For a more pillowy amber, MPEG's Ambre Precieux is excellent, and if the idea of amber conjures up dryer connotations for you, Fort &amp; Manle's Amber Absolutely is worth a try (although I own the original formulation in the black bottle and cannot attest to the quality of the new stuff). But for me, this is where the sidewalk ends on amber, and I'm happy with that. It feels good to reach a destination in a hobby that so often feels like a hamster wheel.<br />
<br />
This one's a 10, no question.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40816"comment_id="1610243"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Grand-Soir-40816.html?ccid=1610243#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2072846" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1438575" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="PhillyFresh"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/189913"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="PhillyFresh" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1438575ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck8x0"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1438575" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/189913">PhillyFresh</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-11-01">11/01/21 17:55</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is seriously a 4/10.<br />
<br />
You can buy middle eastern oils for $5-$10 that smell exactly like this or better. And I'm certain there are much cheaper clones of this that smell more complex and more pleasant.<br />
<br />
With all the hype I've heard for this for the past few years, I expected way more. This scent is pretty blunt, no depth, no nuances. Just simply vanilla and amber. It smells like deep vanilla cupakes. There's nothing really special about it.<br />
<br />
A very easy pass. Nothing interesting about it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40816"comment_id="1438575"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Grand-Soir-40816.html?ccid=1438575#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent947327" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc947327" class="cell small-2" ><div ><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="mimeex"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1130862"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1130862.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="mimeex" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma947327ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck6x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd947327" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1130862">mimeex</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2018-05-28">05/28/18 17:17</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Gorgeous scent. Elegant. Very creamy. It smells like melted butter with amber to me. And it's very simple, easy to wear. Grand Soir lasts very long. It's high quality.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40816"comment_id="947327"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Grand-Soir-40816.html?ccid=947327#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent827429" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc827429" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="fillifelle"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/137867"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.137867.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="fillifelle" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Jil-Sander/Simply-Jil-Sander-Poudree-51719.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.51719.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Simply Jil Sander Poudrée"title="Simply Jil Sander Poudrée"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma827429ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck6x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd827429" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/137867">fillifelle</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2017-05-30">05/30/17 05:35</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I was very excited to try this given how similar the juice looks to APLS, which by the way is a masterpiece of this house. Also because they have the word "soir" in common, I thought I'm in for a luxurious treat. The marketing spiel "Benzoin from Siam (actually Thailand to be politically correct), tonka bean from Brazil, cistus labdanum from Spain" hit all the right spots for me; these are some of my favourite notes!<br />
<br />
Alas, two sentences from a perfume blogger summed this perfume up all too well for me. "The rough synth edge on Grand Soir is unpleasant and harsh/burnt to my nose" and there is a "soullessly chemical side taste" (Takeonethingoff).<br />
<br />
I couldn't agree more. Within ten minutes my frontal lobe was going numb and throbbing from the relentless onslaught of synthetic woody and amber notes. I had to tilt my nose away from the arm to stave off an incipient headache. In fact after writing this review I'm gonna go scrub it off. I know there are many loves for this juice. And I am no ninny when it comes to niche fragrances with a penchant for using aromachemicals and fancy molecules, or even the house of MFK. I deeply love APLS and have the utmost reverence for the iconoclasm of Baccarat Rouge 540. The entire Oud series I find so-so. Grand Soir bears a lot of resemblance to Ormonde Jayne's Tolu, which I can wear. I don't love it though because of the same cloying sickly sweet powdery base. So if you know you're remotely sensitive to some synthetic woods/amber, please do not blind buy. For similar ambers without the negative side effects, try Serge Lutens Ambre Sultan, Maitre Parfumeur et Gantier's Ambre Precieux, or Profumum Roma's Fiori d'Ambra.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40816"comment_id="827429"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Grand-Soir-40816.html?ccid=827429#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1069350" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1141155">cocofluff</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2019-06-11">06/11/19 22:58</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Yup! padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1044143">mermaidylady</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-02-19">02/19/22 11:26</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I got a sample of this thinking, "Amber and vanilla?
